# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="67cfe-102">Membres obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="67cfe-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="67cfe-103">Les tableaux de cet article répertorient les membres de type qui sont obsolètes dans le .NET Framework 4.5 et versions ultérieures, organisées par assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="67cfe-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="67cfe-104">Utilisez les liens suivants pour consulter la liste des membres obsolètes et des alternatives recommandées dans chaque assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="67cfe-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="67cfe-105">Cette rubrique ne répertorie pas les membres des types obsolètes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="67cfe-105">This topic doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="67cfe-106">Pour obtenir la liste des types obsolètes, consultez [Types obsolètes](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="67cfe-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
